# Test Report

Time: 2024-03-30 00:31:29.932160

### Base Program

```py
def countLargestGroup(n: int) -> int:
    groups = [0] * 37
    largest_group_size = 0
    count_largest_groups = 0

    for i in range(1, n + 1):
        sum_of_digits = sum(map(int, str(i)))
        groups[sum_of_digits] += 1
        if groups[sum_of_digits] > largest_group_size:
            largest_group_size = groups[sum_of_digits]
            count_largest_groups = 1
        elif groups[sum_of_digits] == largest_group_size:
            count_largest_groups += 1

    return count_largest_groups
```

### Input

```json
[15]
```

## Test Case 1

### Modified Program

```py
def countLargestGroup(n: int) -> int:
    groups = [0] * 37
    largest_group_size = 0
    count_largest_groups = 0
    for i in range(1, n + 1):
        sum_of_digits = sum(map(int, str(i)))
        groups[sum_of_digits] += 1
        if groups[sum_of_digits] > largest_group_size:
            largest_group_size = groups[sum_of_digits]
            count_largest_groups = 1
        elif groups[sum_of_digits] == largest_group_size:
            count_largest_groups += 1
    return count_largest_groups
```

## Test Case 2

### Modified Program

```py
def countLargestGroup(var_0: int) -> int:
    groups = [0] * 37
    largest_group_size = 0
    count_largest_groups = 0
    for i in range(1, var_0 + 1):
        sum_of_digits = sum(map(int, str(i)))
        groups[sum_of_digits] += 1
        if groups[sum_of_digits] > largest_group_size:
            largest_group_size = groups[sum_of_digits]
            count_largest_groups = 1
        elif groups[sum_of_digits] == largest_group_size:
            count_largest_groups += 1
    return count_largest_groups
```

## Test Case 3

### Modified Program

```py
def countLargestGroup(n: int) -> int:
    groups = 37 * [0]
    largest_group_size = 0
    count_largest_groups = 0
    for i in range(1, 1 + n):
        sum_of_digits = sum(map(int, str(i)))
        groups[sum_of_digits] += 1
        if groups[sum_of_digits] > largest_group_size:
            largest_group_size = groups[sum_of_digits]
            count_largest_groups = 1
        elif groups[sum_of_digits] == largest_group_size:
            count_largest_groups += 1
    return count_largest_groups
```

## Test Case 4

### Modified Program

```py
def countLargestGroup(var_1: int) -> int:
    groups = 37 * [0]
    largest_group_size = 0
    count_largest_groups = 0
    for i in range(1, 1 + var_1):
        sum_of_digits = sum(map(int, str(i)))
        groups[sum_of_digits] += 1
        if groups[sum_of_digits] > largest_group_size:
            largest_group_size = groups[sum_of_digits]
            count_largest_groups = 1
        elif groups[sum_of_digits] == largest_group_size:
            count_largest_groups += 1
    return count_largest_groups
```
